jQuery(\".tab-navigation > li\").eq(index).addClass('active');\n            jQuery(\".pdp-details-nav > dd\").eq(index).addClass('active');\n\n            return false;\n         });\n\n         var connector = function(itemNavigation, carouselStage) {\n            return carouselStage.jcarousel('items').eq(itemNavigation.index());\n         };\n\n         // Setup the carousels. Adjust the options for both carousels here.\n         \n         var carouselStage      = jQuery('.pdp-orbit-container .carousel-stage').jcarousel({\n            wrap: \"circular\"\n         });\n\n         var carouselNavigation = jQuery('.pdp-sub-orbit-container .carousel-navigation').jcarousel({\n            wrap: \"circular\"\n         });\n\n         // We loop through the items of the navigation carousel and set it up\n         // as a control for an item from the stage carousel.\n\n         carouselNavigation.jcarousel('items').each(function() {\n\n            var item = jQuery(this);\n\n            // This is where we actually connect to items.\n\n            var target = connector(item, carouselStage);\n\n            item\n            .on('jcarouselcontrol:active', function() {\n               carouselNavigation.jcarousel('scrollIntoView', this);\n               item.addClass('active');\n            })\n            .on('jcarouselcontrol:inactive', function() {\n               item.removeClass('active');\n            })\n            .jcarouselControl({\n               target: target,\n               carousel: carouselStage\n            });\n\n         });\n\n         // Setup controls for the stage carousel\n\n         jQuery('.prev-stage')\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:inactive', function() {\n            jQuery(this).addClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:active', function() {\n            jQuery(this).removeClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .jcarouselControl({\n            target: '-=1'\n         });\n\n         jQuery('.next-stage')\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:inactive', function() {\n            jQuery(this).addClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:active', function() {\n            jQuery(this).removeClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .jcarouselControl({\n            target: '+=1'\n         });\n\n         // Setup controls for the navigation carousel\n\n         jQuery('.prev-navigation')\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:inactive', function() {\n            jQuery(this).addClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:active', function() {\n            jQuery(this).removeClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .jcarouselControl({\n            target: '-=1'\n         });\n\n         jQuery('.next-navigation')\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:inactive', function() {\n            jQuery(this).addClass('inactive');\n         })\n         .on('jcarouselcontrol:active', function() {\n            jQuery(this).removeClass('inactive'); \n         })\n         .jcarouselControl({\n            target: '+=1'\n         });\n\n         // On resize\n         jQuery(window).resize(function(){\n            jQuery(\".pdp-sub-orbit .active\").click();\n         });\n         \n         \n\n      });\n   </script>\n\n\n\t      \t\t</div>\n\t    \t</div>\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\n\t    \n\t    \n\t    \n\t
